[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis appears to be an **algorithmic complexity vulnerability**, specifically a [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpotential **Denial of Service [0m[1;39m([0m[39mDoS[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m** through computational exhaustion. The fuzzer [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhas likely crafted input that causes the TAR archive parser to perform extremely [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexpensive arithmetic operations, leading to unacceptable processing time.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Key Observations[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Infinite or Near-Infinite Computation**: The thread is stuck in Knuth division[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malgorithm for BigInteger arithmetic, suggesting either very large numbers or a [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpathological case in the division operation.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **PAX Header Timestamp Parsing**: The issue originates from parsing decimal [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mseconds in PAX headers, which uses BigDecimal arithmetic to handle fractional [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mseconds with arbitrary precision.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m82[0m[39m:          <p>A third party can create a malformed TAR file by manipulating file [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmodification times headers, [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m83[0m[39m:             which when parsed with Apache Commons Compress, will cause a denial[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof service issue via CPU consumption.<[0m[35m/[0m[95mp[0m[39m>[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m84[0m[39m:          <p>In version [0m[1;36m1.22[0m[39m of Apache Commons Compress, support was added for [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfile modification times with higher precision [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m85[0m[39m:             [0m[1;39m([0m[39missue # COMPRESS-[0m[1;36m612[0m[39m<sup><a [0m[33mhref[0m[39m=[0m[32m"#Ref-1-24-1"[0m[39m>[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95ma[0m[39m><[0m[35m/[0m[95msup[0m[39m>[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m86[0m[39m:             The format for the PAX extended headers carrying this data consists[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof two numbers separated by a period<sup><a [0m[33mhref[0m[39m=[0m[32m"#Ref-1-24-2"[0m[39m>[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m][0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95ma[0m[39m><[0m[35m/[0m[95msup[0m[39m>, [0m      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m89[0m[39m:          <p>Parsing of these numbers uses the BigDecimal<sup><a [0m                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Core Issue Analysis[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe root cause of this timeout is a **BigDecimal algorithmic complexity [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerability** in the PAX header timestamp parsing logic. The issue occurs in [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mTarArchiveEntry.parseInstantFromDecimalSeconds[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` where:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Vulnerable Regex Pattern** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m221[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m222[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: The pattern `-?\d[0m[1;39m{[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m19[0m[1;39m}[0m[1;39m([0m[39m?:\.\d*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m?` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrectly limits the integer part to [0m[1;36m19[0m[39m digits but allows **unlimited decimal [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdigits** with `[0m[1;39m([0m[39m?:\.\d*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m?`[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Expensive BigDecimal Operation** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m277[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: When a malicious input like [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[32m"1."[0m[39m` followed by [0m[1;36m300[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m000[0m[39m decimal digits is provided:[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The regex validation passes[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - A BigDecimal is created with extremely high precision[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `[0m[1;35mremainder[0m[1;39m([0m[39mBigDecimal.ONE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` operation triggers Knuth division algorithm in[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBigInteger[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - CPU consumption becomes exponential, causing the timeout[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Known Vulnerability**: The security documentation confirms this is a [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdocumented DoS vulnerability [0m[1;39m([0m[39msimilar to CVE-[0m[1;36m2012[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m2098[0m[39m, referencing JDK-[0m[1;36m6560193[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat affects versions [0m[1;36m1.22[0m[39m onwards.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Fix Implementation[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Primary Fix: Update the Regex Pattern**[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mModify `TarArchiveEntry.java` line [0m[1;36m221[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m222[0m[39m to limit the fractional part to a [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaximum of [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m decimal digits [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnanosecond precision[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprivate static final Pattern PAX_EXTENDED_[0m[1;33mHEAD[0m[39mER_FILE_TIMES_PATTERN =[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mPattern.compile[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"-?\\d[0m[32m{[0m[32m1,19[0m[32m}[0m[32m([0m[32m?:\\.\\d[0m[32m{[0m[32m1,9[0m[32m}[0m[32m)[0m[32m?"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Changes:**[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Change `[0m[1;39m([0m[39m?:\\.\\d*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m?` to `[0m[1;39m([0m[39m?:\\.\\d[0m[1;39m{[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m9[0m[1;39m}[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m?`[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This enforces [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m9[0m[39m decimal digits when a decimal point is present[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Allows [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m decimal digits if no decimal point [0m[1;39m([0m[39minteger timestamps[0m[1;39m)[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why This is Optimal:**[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Prevents DoS Attack**: Limits fractional part to [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m digits, preventing creation[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof BigDecimals with pathological precision that trigger expensive arithmetic [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperations[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Preserves Legitimate Use Cases**:[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Java's `[0m[1;35mInstant.ofEpochSecond[0m[1;39m([0m[39mseconds, nanos[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` supports nanosecond precision [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[1;36m9[0m[39m decimal digits[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Real-world PAX timestamps use [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m decimal digits [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m[32m"1647221103.5998539"[0m[39m in [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtests[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The limit of [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m digits accommodates maximum meaningful precision[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Aligns with Write Logic**: [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mTarArchiveOutputStream.addInstantPaxHeader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` writes timestamps with [0m[33mscale[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m7[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The read path should accept at least what the write path produces[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Maintains Existing Validation**:[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Still rejects exponent notation [0m[1;39m([0m[32m"9e9999999"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - no [0m[32m'e'[0m[39m or [0m[32m'E'[0m[39m in pattern[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Still limits integer part to [0m[1;36m19[0m[39m digits[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Still requires at least [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m digit in integer part[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Minimal Code Change**: Single-line fix to the regex pattern, no changes to [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic flow[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Logic[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Critical Logic Preserved:**[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Error Handling** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m280[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m283[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: The try-catch block for `DateTimeException` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand `ArithmeticException` remains intact to handle overflow cases[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **BigDecimal Operations** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m275[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m277[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: The arithmetic logic remains [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munchanged:[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Extract seconds as long value[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Calculate nanoseconds from fractional part[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - These operations are safe when precision is bounded[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Validation Flow** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m271[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m273[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Pattern matching still occurs before [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBigDecimal creation[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **PAX Header Processing** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1602[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1613[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: The routing of timestamp headers to[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mparseInstantFromDecimalSeconds[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` remains unchanged[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Test Compatibility**: [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Valid timestamps in tests have ≤[0m[1;36m7[0m[39m decimal digits - will still pass[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Invalid values [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexponent notation, out-of-range[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - will still fail correctly[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**No Impact on Broader Codebase:**[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Change is localized to one constant definition[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No changes to method signatures or return types[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No changes to exception handling[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No changes to other header processing logic[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No changes to utility methods like `ParsingUtils`[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Alternative Approaches Considered[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Alternative [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Length Check Before BigDecimal Creation**[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mvalue.length[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m > [0m[1;36m30[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Corrupted PAX header. Time field value is too long"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Rejected**: Less precise than limiting decimal digits; doesn't prevent [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"1.000000000000000000001"[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m21[0m[39m chars, [0m[1;36m20[0m[39m decimal digits[0m[1;39m)[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Alternative [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Manual String Parsing**[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Parse integer and fractional parts separately without BigDecimal[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Rejected**: More complex implementation; BigDecimal is safe when precision is [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbounded[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Alternative [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Limit Total String Length**[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Check `[0m[1;35mvalue.length[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` before regex[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Rejected**: Doesn't address the root cause [0m[1;39m([0m[39munlimited decimal digits[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m; [0m[32m"1."[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m9[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdigits is [0m[1;36m11[0m[39m chars, [0m[32m"1."[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m300[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m000[0m[39m digits is [0m[1;36m300[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m002[0m[39m chars[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Alternative [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m: Catch Timeout in BigDecimal Operations**[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Wrap operations with timeout mechanism[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Rejected**: Band-aid solution; doesn't prevent the expensive operation from [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstarting[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m. Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential Side Effects:**[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Rejection of Timestamps with >[0m[1;36m9[0m[39m Decimal Digits**:[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Impact**: Extremely rare - no legitimate use case needs more than nanosecond[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprecision[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: [0m[3;35mNone[0m[39m needed - this is intentional security hardening[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Breaking Change for Malicious Archives**:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Impact**: Archives crafted to exploit the vulnerability will now fail to [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparse[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: This is the desired behavior[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**No Breaking Changes for Legitimate Use:**[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. All test cases pass [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m7[0m[39m decimal digits in valid tests[0m[1;39m)[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Maximum meaningful precision preserved [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m9[0m[39m decimal digits = nanoseconds[0m[1;39m)[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Integer-only timestamps still supported [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno decimal point[0m[1;39m)[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. PAX standard compliance maintained[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m. Testing Considerations[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix should be validated against:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Existing Tests**: All current tests should pass unchanged[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mcreateEntryForTimeTests[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` uses [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m decimal digits - will pass[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mtestPaxTimeFieldsForInvalidValues[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` tests exponent notation - will pass[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Attack Vectors** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfrom security.xml[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Long fraction: [0m[32m"1."[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m300[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m000[0m[39m digits - should be REJECTED[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Exponent notation: [0m[32m"9e9999999"[0m[39m - already REJECTED[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Boundary Cases**:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m decimal digits: [0m[32m"1.123456789"[0m[39m - should PASS[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m decimal digits: [0m[32m"1.1234567890"[0m[39m - should be REJECTED[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Integer only: [0m[32m"1234567890"[0m[39m - should PASS[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Zero decimals with point: [0m[32m"1."[0m[39m - should be REJECTED [0m[1;39m([0m[39mrequires at least [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m digit[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mafter point[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m. Implementation Notes[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**File to Modify:**[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/tar/TarArchiveEntry.java`[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Line to Change:**[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m222[0m[39m: Change `[0m[1;35mPattern.compile[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"-?\\d[0m[32m{[0m[32m1,19[0m[32m}[0m[32m([0m[32m?:\\.\\d*[0m[32m)[0m[32m?"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` to [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mPattern.compile[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"-?\\d[0m[32m{[0m[32m1,19[0m[32m}[0m[32m([0m[32m?:\\.\\d[0m[32m{[0m[32m1,9[0m[32m}[0m[32m)[0m[32m?"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**No Other Files Need Modification:**[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No changes to harness code [0m[1;39m([0m[39mCompressTarFuzzer.java[0m[1;39m)[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No changes to test files[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No changes to TarFile.java, TarUtils.java, or other parsing logic[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No changes to utility classes[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix directly addresses the security vulnerability documented in the codebase [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhile maintaining full backward compatibility with legitimate use cases.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
